<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возглавлять.html>возглавля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozglavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возглавить.html>возгла́вить</a></b>)

<ol><li>to lead, to head, to be at head

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возглавлять.html>возглавля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экспедиция.html>экспеди́цию</a></i><sup id="cite_ref-словопидия-вожглавлять_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-словопидия-вожглавлять-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozglavljátʹ</b> ekspedíciju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead an expedition</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возглавлять.html>возглавля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йско</a></i><sup id="cite_ref-словопидия-вожглавлять_1-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-словопидия-вожглавлять-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozglavljátʹ</b> vójsko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead an army</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возгорание.html>возгора́ние</a> (31697)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">возгора́ть(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozgorátʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возгорание.html>возгора́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozgoránije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возгорание.html>возгора́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возгорание.html>возгора́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возгорание.html>возгора́ний</a></b>)

***воздавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздавать.html>воздава́ть</a> (29967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздать.html>возда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozdátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздавать.html>воздава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozdavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздать.html>возда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to render, to do (something) in recognition of something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воздавать.html>воздава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>до́лжное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozdavátʹ</b> dólžnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to render tribute, to give (somebody or something) their due</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воздавать.html>воздава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почесть.html>по́чести</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozdavátʹ</b> póčesti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give honors to, to pay homage to <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to repay, to reward, to recompense <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental of thing repaid</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воздавать.html>воздава́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добро́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozdavátʹ</b> dobróm za zlo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to repay good for evil, to repay evil with good</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***воздать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздать.html>возда́ть</a> (20647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздать.html>возда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozdátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздавать.html>воздава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to render, to do (something) in recognition of something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воздать.html>возда́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:должный.html>до́лжное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozdátʹ</b> dólžnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to render tribute, to give (somebody or something) their due</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воздать.html>возда́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почесть.html>по́чести</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozdátʹ</b> póčesti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give honors to, to pay homage to <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to repay, to reward, to recompense <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental of thing repaid</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:воздать.html>возда́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добро́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>зло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozdátʹ</b> dobróm za zlo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to repay good for evil, to repay evil with good</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздействие.html>возде́йствие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozdéjstvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздействие.html>возде́йствия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздействие.html>возде́йствия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздействие.html>возде́йствий</a></b>)

***воздержавшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздержаться.html>воздержа́вшийся</a> (10166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздержаться.html>воздержа́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozderžávšijsja</span>)

***воздух.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>воздух</a> (343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въздоухъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭzduxŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vózdux</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здуха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здухи</a></i>, <i>genitive plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здухов</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> air</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> air, atmosphere</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> money</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воззвание.html>воззва́ние</a> (27047)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воззвать.html>воззва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozzvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воззвание.html>воззва́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozzvánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воззвание.html>воззва́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воззвание.html>воззва́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воззвание.html>воззва́ний</a></b>)
</p>
